Shen Bao Amateur Weekly

Amateur Anecdotes

The Gold Disaster in America

— Wang Yuanfang

Everyone knows that the United States is the world's gold country. According to recent statistics, the total gold reserves of central banks in various countries around the world are approximately US$21.67 billion, of which the United States accounts for 45 percent. This means that the United States now owns almost half of the world's gold. At the same time, since the beginning of September this year, European gold has been constantly flowing to the United States, causing it to increase by several million or tens of millions of dollars of huge gold reserves almost every day. As a result, the total gold owned by the United States has broken through 9.5 billion U.S. dollars. Therefore, some people in financial circles have issued a cry for a "gold disaster." The "Shen Bao" on January 24th once contained the following piece of news: "According to a recent report from the US Treasury Department, the total value of gold reserves in the United States is £1,960,000,000, and even more continues to be shipped in. Since September, the inflow of gold from abroad has amounted to £125,000,000, of which £72,000,000 came from France, £30,000 from the United Kingdom, and £12,000,000 from the Netherlands. The public is not without concern about the continuous inflow of gold, because gold that has no use has now filled the banks, and if large amounts of gold continue to flow in, it is feared that it will help to promote the rise of latent lending and expansion." From this, it can be seen that the so-called cry for a "gold disaster" is not without reason.

In fact, since the devaluation of the US dollar at the end of January last year, the total gold owned by the United States has shown the following increasing trend.

(Unit: Millions of US Dollars)

End of January last year 6,829

End of December last year 8,8,138

End of August this year 9,197

Mid-October this year 9,584

From the above table, it can be seen that from November last year to mid-October this year, the total gold owned by the United States has increased by more than 2 billion US dollars. The sources of these gold are as follows:

(Unit: Millions of US Dollars)

From France 838

From the United Kingdom 747

From the Netherlands 318

From Canada 160

From India 123

From other places 167

Total 2,353

Originally, in the past, European countries still had the return flow of American capital escaping overseas, but recently, most of the gold in Europe has flowed to the United States to seek refuge due to the unrest in the European political situation and the shaking of the gold bloc. As for the inflow of Indian gold to the United States, it has come with the soaring gold prices.

It seems very strange, but the gold that flowed into the United States from the United Kingdom in the past was not the United Kingdom's own gold, but mainly European continental capital that flowed to the United States through the United Kingdom. From January last year to August this year, the movement of gold in the United Kingdom had a surplus of 138 million pounds to the United States, but its overall surplus was 27 million pounds. The details are as follows:

(Unit: Millions of Pounds)

Inflow from France 96

Inflow from the Netherlands 13

Inflow from India 60

Inflow from South Africa 100

Outflow 62

Surplus from inflow and outflow 207

However, the situation has been different since September this year. A lot of gold from the United Kingdom directly or through France has also flowed into the United States. As a result, in the six weeks from the end of August to October 10, a surplus of 9.8 million pounds was created. The details are as follows:

(Unit: Millions of Pounds)

Detailed amount of import 19.0

From South Africa 10.0

From India 5.7

From France 0.7

From the Netherlands 1.0

Total amount of export 28.8

To the United States 22.3

To France 1.8

However, because there was more gold inflow in the past, the recent increase in gold outflow from the United Kingdom is not a big deal. At the same time, the outflow of gold from the United Kingdom has gradually decreased in the past two weeks. According to reports, "In the week ending on the 13th, the export of gold from the United Kingdom decreased compared with the previous week, and the import increased. The total export amount was £2,927,000, a decrease of £2,052,000 compared with the previous week, of which £830,000 was shipped to the United States, £358,000 to the Netherlands, £511,000 to Sweden, £213,000 to Germany, and £117,000 to France. The total import amount was £2,875,000, coming from Africa, £1820,000, India £950,000, France £1,126,000, Germany £126,000." In addition, the export of gold from the United Kingdom continued to decrease in the week ending on the 20th. Its total export amount was £1,783,000, a decrease of £1,144,000 compared with the previous week. The total import amount was £11,987,000, and the net import was £1,204,000, an increase of £1,156,000 compared with the previous week. From this, it can be seen that the recent increase in gold exports from the United Kingdom is not as great as the situation since September. However, the gold exported from the United Kingdom still flows into the United States directly or indirectly, so the import of gold in the United States does not stop increasing due to the decrease in exports from the United Kingdom.

Among the world's gold flowing into the United States, France is particularly noteworthy. Originally, France's gold reserves accounted for 22 percent of the world's total, second only to the United States. At the same time, when various countries around the world abandoned the gold standard one after another, France still worked hard to maintain it and formed a gold bloc to compete with the US dollar and the pound sterling. However, recently, due to the increasingly sharp struggle between the left and right extremes in the country and the development of economic and political crises, a large amount of cash in France, the world's second largest gold country, has flowed out. The report on November 16th said: "Since the Bank of France issued its weekly report last Wednesday, a large amount of gold has continued to flow out of the country. The bank then raised the discount rate again this month, from 5% to 6%, in order to remedy the situation. It is estimated that since November 14, more than 100,000 francs of domestic gold have flowed out of the country. The government will formally announce this figure on Wednesday. It is expected that the amount of gold and silver currency listed in the Bank of France's weekly report will decrease from 700 million francs to 690 million francs. ... The current level of gold reserves of 690 million francs is similar to the amount of inventory in 1931." Such a large amount of gold, of course, is mostly flowing into the United States. Judging from the current situation, French gold may continue to flow out, so American gold will continue to increase.

However, gold is fluid. If you have a large amount of gold but have no use for it, it will attract disasters. The United States is currently facing the danger of inflation due to the large inflow of gold and the increase in the issuance of silver certificates. The excess reserves of various banks have now reached 3 billion US dollars, and the interest rate still shows an unprecedentedly low level. This is very good for the general industry, but not good for banks that are working hard to improve their profitability. At the same time, the increase in excess reserves poses a risk of currency inflation. A recent bank monthly report in the United States issued such a warning: "The inflow of gold into the United States does not get any lasting benefits, because the capital that flows in rapidly may flow out rapidly in the future. Moreover, gold is now useless and threatening." The report also pointed out that the current reserve of US banks has risen to an extremely high number, so the increase in gold will cause the danger of expansion.

The world is like this. Some countries have dry finances and lack cash, while others have too much gold and are in danger. The "gold disaster" in the United States is a manifestation of the latter, which is a malformed manifestation in the era of capitalist decline.

Art World

Review of "Boat Girl"

— Chen Shuxun

I remember that in the "May Fourth" era, a group of knowledgeable women actually participated in the "women's liberation movement." At the same time, they loudly shouted anti-feudal slogans such as "equal employment for women," "free marriage for women," and "economic independence for women." From the May Fourth Movement to now, there has been fifteen or sixteen years of history. In this not-short process, to what extent has the liberation of Chinese women reached? According to my personal observation, apart from a few knowledgeable women who have obtained the status of "vase" and , the rest are either still slaves in the family or have embarked on the fate of a boat girl, A-Ling - prostitution.

What is the reason for this? "Boat Girl" hints in its prologue that men and women who are working hard for the women's liberation movement shout slogans that are earth-shattering, and do a lot of publicity, but they (or she) themselves are either demons who play with women or tools to be played with by others, just as the prologue says: Enthusiastic ladies send out beautiful high energies, the slogan of prostitutes is loud and clear, what is the soul after the meeting ,Taiwanese dance ambitions , the author is firmly grasping , At the same time, the ridicule and satire given are also reasonable and should be done. Although the main reason for the failure of the women's liberation movement has not been proposed or hinted at by the playwright.

Perhaps because of the playwright's rich feelings, several scenes are full of emotional atmosphere, and the characters in the play are so enthusiastic and unrestrained. For example, the close attitude and mutual aid spirit between Tie Er and his daughter A-Ling are worthy of praise and admiration. At the same time, after Tie Er discovered that A-Ling had sneaked into his house at night and understood the "mystery" of the past (A-Ling quietly mended his clothes and cooked his meals), the surprise and the shy posture of the young girl A-Ling all showed a kind of unstoppable enthusiasm; although they did not say a word, all the infinite things in their hearts were unsaid, and the power of emotion was greater than a thousand words. When A-Ling shyly ran away, Tie Er's ecstatic action (ecstatic jumping) was especially the point where his emotions swelled to the boiling point. I think this scene is the most exciting, the most tense, the most relaxing, and the most able to grab the audience's heart. These are all the irrigation of the playwright's enthusiasm. However, precisely because the emotions are too rich, if they are allowed to develop wildly, they can distort reason. For example, after A-Ling was forced into prostitution, Tie Er found her in the brothel. The way they were so affectionate was of course very touching. At the same time, it was quite pleasant to be so angry that he madly beat the prostitutes and made trouble in the brothel, but this can only be said to be a personal heroic performance. You must know that those who create sin are not the prostitutes, nor are they the pimps and procuresses who open brothels. It is impossible to eliminate sin and solve problems by merely grieving and venting anger or making a fuss.

In addition, there are one or two minor flaws: First, small boats often have business competition and conflicts when soliciting passengers. This situation is very common whether at the ferry crossing or on the lake where there are many tourists. If we go to Xuanwu Lake, as soon as we arrive at the dam entrance, the voices of people soliciting passengers will be earth-shattering, and they will even grab us. However, the small boats on the lake in "Boat Girl" do not have this phenomenon. Although A-Ling and her father shouted "Go to Yue Fei's tomb," it was such a brief sound, two sounds, which lacked the meaning of life panic. Second, regarding their residence, I think the environment is too beautiful, especially where Tie Er lives. The inside is so "bright and clean," and the outside is surrounded by big trees and small bamboos. If you don't say it is the residence of a weaver, I would mistakenly think it is a "study" of a poet and writer!

Life Guidance

How to Manipulate a Group

— Xiong Zi

In the cave-dwelling era, there was no society at all, so there was no organization to speak of. Later, as people had more and more opportunities to interact, societies gradually formed in order to protect common interests. In modern times, science has flourished, and human interactions have become more frequent. Whether in politics, business, or private enterprises, organizations need to be well-organized and managed scientifically in order to achieve results and success. Therefore, it can be said that group organization is unique to human beings, whose intelligence surpasses all other creatures. It can also be said that group organization is a symbol of civilization and progress.

The benefits of organization are many. Here are some of the most important ones:

First, the spirit of one person, even a sage, hero, or outstanding individual, is always limited. Complex affairs can never be handled by one person alone, and no single person can possess all knowledge and abilities. Therefore, it is necessary for many people to cooperate and manage together in order to shoulder significant responsibilities.

Second, the conference system is now popular as a substitute for the dictatorial system. It can avoid the prejudice of one person and achieve the effect of collecting wisdom and benefiting from the collective. precise organization facilitates division of labor and enables everyone to use their talents to the fullest. The result of the implementation of scientific management in modern industry is rapid action and increased production. The workers in each department are like machines that are interconnected. The person in charge uses the workers like moving machines. The Ford Motor Company in the United States is a world-famous factory, and its output is extremely astonishing. The reason why it can achieve such results is directly due to the wonderful use of division of labor and cooperation, and indirectly due to the gift of precise organization.

Fourth, having an organization can cultivate a life of discipline. A life of discipline gradually becomes a habit. After an action becomes a habit, many energies can be saved invisibly. A person's energy is limited. Being able to save energies that can be saved and devote them to the advancement of one's career will naturally have much better results.

Fifth, with precise organization and division of labor, it is possible to select people for tasks and enable those with special skills and talents to have the opportunity to develop, so as to avoid the sigh of "a hero with no place to use his talents."

There are two elements of organization: one is "affairs," and the other is "people." To manipulate a group, both "affairs" and "people" must be fully utilized for our benefit. If one is missing, it will inevitably fail.

The following principles should be followed when manipulating affairs:

(1) System - People who act as leaders, because affairs are clustered, if there is no systematic handling, on the one hand, they will inevitably be exhausted from handling trivial affairs, and on the other hand, because they are trapped by trivial branch matters, they will inevitably be hindered from their talents and cannot free themselves.

(2) Utilization - There are two things that can be utilized in handling affairs: 1. Machines should be utilized at any time. There are two benefits: A' saves time, and B, the effect is better than manual labor; 2. Within the possible scope, office workers from each department should be utilized at any time to assign tasks.

Below we will further discuss the method of manipulating affairs:

(1) Analysis of affairs:

A. Classification - Summarize the various complicated affairs into several categories: such as "unfinished affairs," "letters," telegrams," "telephone calls," "visitors," etc.

B. Grading - Divide affairs into grades according to their importance and urgency. For example, taking importance as the standard, there are important, routine, and social letters. Should we distinguish which ones should be returned to the file, which ones should be prepared for examination, and which ones can be drafted by assistants? Which ones should be handled by yourself? Those that take urgency as the standard should of course be handled first, and those that can be postponed should be temporarily postponed to avoid repayment.

(2) Use of machines:

How should affairs be managed? How can management be considered superior? If a person is organized, he must be able to think comprehensively and avoid acting blindly. And when it comes to handling affairs, he can use various machines to help him handle affairs, so as to achieve an orderly effect.

There are many machines that can be used to handle affairs. Here are a few:

(1) Desk - Drawers are divided into "filed files" and "to-do items."

(2) Memorandum - Either use a book or a loose-leaf page, depending on convenience. It is also possible to use a calendar card as a memorandum. If it is applicable, it is also acceptable.

(3) File box - The boxes are divided into columns, marked with identification. When inspecting, take them from the drawer of the column listed in the saddle. It is very convenient.

In addition, such things as a call bell, business card index, blank forms, charts, etc. are all indispensable supplies for handling affairs.

(3) Assignment of people:

Complicated personnel affairs cannot be solely responsible for or handled by one person alone. Robinson was indeed able to maintain his life independently on a deserted island, but after all, that way of life was very primitive. From a modern perspective, this method is extremely rare in practice and extremely uneconomical in principle. Because people's intelligence is different, the things that each person can do must also be different. For example, engineers must be able to produce scientific and artistic drawings, and civil construction workers must be able to build houses according to the drawings made by engineers. Each person's job is different. If you force an engineer to draw drawings and then build houses himself, let alone whether the houses he builds are his expertise, he will waste his time, which is an extremely uneconomical method.

Those who are good at handling things do not necessarily have to "do everything themselves," but must be good at assigning others. Even if you are a hero, your energy is limited. If you do everything yourself and waste too much energy, it will be harmful rather than beneficial. Napoleon was a rare hero, and his energy was also superior to others. He did not give up on small matters, and he took on everything himself. But how long did it take for his energy to gradually decline? In the Battle of Leipzig, one person's strength was insufficient, and the subordinates had not been trained at ordinary times, so they suffered a heavy blow.

Therefore, the way to handle affairs should be like an arm using a hand, like a hand using a finger. If the fingers are used properly, things will succeed.

Page 19

(4) Handling of routine matters:

Every day when you walk into the office, there are many routine tasks waiting for you to handle. You should not only "suit" these routine tasks, but also "be swift."

The first step is to check the "unfinished affairs" recorded in the temporary record and deal with them first.

The second step is to check the tasks listed in the schedule for today and handle them.

The third step is to deal with new events.

When dealing with new events, pay attention to the clarity of the organization. For example, (1) those that must be handled immediately should be classified as urgent. (2) Those that require people to handle them should be classified as commissioned. (3) If they are to be reviewed, they should be listed in the temporary file box, so that they are well-organized and not chaotic in the slightest.

Amateur Study

Methods of Studying Geography and Political Geography

— Ms. Qing Tang

When we were in primary and secondary school, besides English and arithmetic, the most convenient and rigid subject in our studies was probably geography. The so-called geography textbooks at that time were full of names and locations of mountains, deserts, railways, cities, oceans, rivers, harbors, straits, islands, etc. Geography teachers, of course, only knew how to "hold a book and follow the textbook and map, forcing students to memorize countless place names and their shapes; as for the exams? It goes without saying that they were based on the teacher's teaching and the students' learning, with questions asking how many islands there were in the Pacific Ocean, their names and locations, or how high the Himalayas were, or how long the Andes were. How could such a study of geography not make people feel that geography is a very boring subject?

In fact, the content of geography is not so simple and rigid. Generally speaking, all geographical features and natural phenomena, and their relationship with human life, are the objects of geographical study. Therefore, studying geography is not just about memorizing place names and their locations, or even just memorizing all natural phenomena and geographical features, but rather understanding the reasons behind them and their relationship to human life. For example, to understand how the rainy season in Abyssinia comes about, why day and night are completely opposite in the Western and Eastern Hemispheres, why the North and South Poles have half a year of daylight and half a year of night, and the reasons for solar and lunar eclipses and the rise and fall of tides, one must have knowledge of "astronomy above" and "geography below." Furthermore, in explaining the relationship between the Yellow River and the Yangtze River and past Chinese civilization, and in explaining the role of the Nile River in ancient Egyptian civilization, one must have knowledge of geography, history, and sociology. Moreover, if one only memorizes that the Danube is the second longest river in Europe, passing through eight countries including Switzerland, Germany, Austria, Hungary, Czechoslovakia, Yugoslavia, Bulgaria, and Romania, and flowing into the Black Sea, that is naturally very simple and rigid. But if one wants to understand the conflicts between France, Germany, Italy, Austria-Hungary, and the Little Entente countries, and even England, etc., on the Danube, that becomes very complex and interesting; but besides knowing the geographical features of the Danube, one must also understand political economics and the political situation in the Danube basin. Based on these facts, we believe that geography is indeed a very complex and important subject; studying geography requires not only memory, but also understanding, and the ability to use common sense from various disciplines to understand all geographical features and natural phenomena.

Does this mean that studying geography is more difficult than anything else? However, when we say that studying geography requires common sense from various disciplines, we do not mean that you should conduct a thorough study of all disciplines, but rather that you should acquire a certain degree of general knowledge from various disciplines in order to understand geographical features and natural phenomena. For example, when understanding the phenomenon of half a year of daylight and half a year of night at the North and South Poles, you only need to know the shape of the Earth and its rotation in relation to day and night on Earth, and you don't need to become a dedicated astronomer. In fact, all disciplines are interconnected, and studying any subject requires a considerable amount of knowledge from other disciplines. For example, someone who studies history must have considerable knowledge of sociology, anthropology, geography, political economics, and so on. The same is true for anyone who studies any other discipline.

At the same time, although the Earth exists objectively outside our minds, all geographical features and natural phenomena are directly or indirectly related to our lives. The ability of rivers and oceans to facilitate our transportation, the difficulty of mountains and deserts in allowing us to travel, the hindrance of typhoons and torrential rains to our navigation, and the benefits of natural products from various places to our lives are all clear evidence of the close relationship between geographical features and natural phenomena and human life. We study geography not just to memorize some place names, but mainly to understand the relationship between geography and human life, and thereby use this geographical knowledge to strive to promote the evolution of the relationship between humans and nature, in order to continuously improve our lives. Therefore, in addition to conducting general surveys of geography, we must especially study it from the perspective of the relationship between human life and geography. For the sake of convenience, we will divide this into three aspects—

(1) How to study geographical features? Regarding geographical features, the main thing, of course, is to understand them in relation to the country, the nation, and human society. For example, when studying the situation of the Balkan Peninsula, it is of course necessary to know that it protrudes between the Black Sea and the Mediterranean Sea, holding the throat of Asia and Europe, but if we do not study the conflicts between England, Russia, Germany, France, Italy, and Austria there before the war, and do not study the domestic situations of England, France, Italy, and the Little Entente countries after the war, as well as their political and even military relations with this region, then knowing that the Balkans have such geographical features is useless. This is because the current geographical importance of the Balkans is formed under the complex political relations of the European powers, and if the complex and serious political situation of the Balkans is not understood, then its important geographical features cannot be understood. In addition, when studying the situation of the Pacific Ocean, the situation of the Baltic Sea, the situation of the Danube basin..., it is necessary to know the economic, political, and even military relations of certain countries in these places in order to understand why their geographical features are important. The reason has been stated above.

(2) Research on the climate of various places. As humanity has evolved to the present, the cold and heat of the climate can no longer directly and absolutely affect people's lives, and using the cold and heat of the climate to explain the characteristics of various peoples is an exaggerated expression of the effect of nature. However, the fact that the climate can affect the survival of plants and animals, and still has more or less influence on human life, is undeniable. Moreover, even now, the climate in some places is still resisting human power. For example, although the North and South Poles have now been explored by humans, because their climate is too cold, and it is half a year of daylight and half a year of night, it is still not easy for humans to live there, and the abundant products there have not all been developed to help human life. Because of these relationships, when we study the geography and climate of a place, in addition to knowing the climate situation of a certain place and why it has that climate, we should also know what items its climate is suitable for producing, and what relationship it has with the lives of the local people; if the climate of a certain place is too cold or too hot, hindering human life, then we should go further to conquer it. Only by studying the climate of geography in this way can it benefit human life, otherwise, it is of little use to simply know that a certain place is cold, a certain place is cool, and a certain place is warm.

(3) Research on the products of various places. It goes without saying that products have a more direct relationship with human life. Therefore, the study of products in various places should of course be linked to the relationship with human life. However, in the meantime, we should pay special attention to the relationship between the products of various places and various countries, because this can also give us some international knowledge. For example, the oil mines in Abyssinia have become the reason for the struggle between England, Italy, and even the United States for Abyssinia; the struggle between Germany and France for Alsace-Lorraine and the Rhine River is because these places produce abundant coal and iron; if we want to study the products of these places, we must know their international relations.

Studying geography in this way can not only acquire useful geographical knowledge, but also increase general knowledge. Without saying anything else, if you do not study geography according to this method, and do not know the national situation of Italy, the relationship between England and Italy in East Africa and the Mediterranean, and all the circumstances of Abyssinia, then you will still not understand the significance of the Italian-Abyssinian War when you see it in the newspaper. It can be seen from this that studying geography in this way is also beneficial for reading newspapers.

Now, political geography is highly valued. For example, articles about the Mediterranean, the Strait of Gibraltar, the Suez Canal, and the Nile River, which are published in various magazines and newspapers, are all called political geography. Recently, there have been publications of books and maps on political geography. This kind of geography is interesting and not rigid to study, and the results can also obtain a lot of useful knowledge, which is much better than the boring geography of the past. But this kind of political geography is based on the research methods mentioned above.

Amateur Coffee Shop

Talking About Prostitutes

— Gui

I have traveled a lot of China's land. Wherever I go, whether it is a big or small city or a town or village, I can see more or less some pale-faced women who are malnourished and sleep-deprived. They are either throwing glances at others or twisting their bodies to flaunt their charm. This cannot be said to be "romantic" or "flirtatious," but rather full of life's anxieties! If these kinds of women are also members of society, then there are too many such people in the current society. This doesn't seem like a good phenomenon!

Scraps of Brocade

Li Liweng's Aphorisms

— Zhou Leshan

Although I am very poor and humble, I would never dare to do anything that sacrifices integrity for profit: rather drag a long skirt today than climb over the wall to steal tiles back then.

Inkstones are not beautiful or ugly, the one that grinds ink well is good. The reason why Duanxi inkstones are valued is because they can grind ink well; if they only have the name of Duanxi but not the reality of grinding ink, it is like Xishi being a barren woman, and Pan An being a eunuch.

Last year, due to migration, I borrowed two hundred taels of gold from a military man. The cruelty of his dunning was a hundred times worse than a Rakshasa. Half of it has been repaid these days, so it can be said that half of him is human and half is a ghost.

My ears burned last night. Could it be that some hooligans were again slandering me with beautiful women? The reason why I incurred the wrath of the hooligans was because the clowns I portrayed in my humble dramas were so similar to these people that they were later brutally murdered, hence the sadness of a fox or rabbit. As for the beautiful women, I have no virtue or resentment towards them. Why don't they discern the cause and effect and echo them? Is it any wonder that I rarely use their beautiful names in my miscellaneous dramas? Perhaps they are pre-emptively getting angry, planning to be portrayed in the future? In solitude during the journey, I enjoy talking to myself. As the saying goes, "Adding a guest doesn't require killing a chicken," especially since there are no chickens to kill anyway, so it's just adding some sinew and increasing the cup.

After leaving home, I remembered one thing: the wall on the east side is very thin, which is a shortcut for burglars; moreover, the servants are fond of sleeping, so it is difficult to expect them to be watchdogs.

The price of rice in Ganzhou is cheaper than chaff in my Zhejiang. Even now, after moving to Baimen, the price of rice is slightly cheaper than in Zhejiang, but eating here is still more frugal than drinking porridge in Jinling. It makes me think that travelers want to eat their fill and die, while family members want to starve to death. How can the difference between sweetness and bitterness be so uneven?

Nothing is lacking during the journey, even to the point of several people sharing one bed. The coolness is bearable, but the heat is really unbearable. I have to borrow from Chen Fan's house, whether it is bamboo or wood. Fortunately, I can borrow one of them, so there is no need to say that I won't go down unless it's Xu Ru.

Asking people for flowers is an elegant affair for oneself, but not for the other person. However, not asking my old man for purple flowers is inelegant for myself, and not an elegant affair for my old man either.

Yesterday, an old man reported across the river that your department's grapes were ripe and wanted to pick them for me. My family members have been drooling for a whole day and night. Now that they have been delivered, eating them feels even more delicious, because they have been desired for a long time and then obtained, which is different from suddenly encountering them. This is the same as marrying a plum blossom at the beginning and passing the imperial examination with white hair. Thank you.

I have been in Chu for half a year, and I have gained very little money, but I have gained quite a few sentences.

Are there any people in the world who are poorer than Liweng on the lake? Everyone says yes. There are so many poor people in the world that they exceed the sands of the Ganges. They all suffer from a lack of fixed property, little business, and no one to rely on in all directions. Even if there is someone to rely on, it is not much. They lack the gift of a coarse silk robe in the cold and have no one to ask for rice when hungry. This is why they are poor. I do not have the fields that eight mouths should have, but there are five times as many people who are waiting for me to provide for them. Even if there are articles that can be sold, the money from selling articles can be counted on one's fingers. With forty mouths relying on one person for food, it is like one mulberry leaf feeding a hundred baskets of silkworms. They grow day and night, how can it be enough?

West Lake is nothing else but the Song Dynasty's pond for releasing animals; today's so-called pond for releasing animals is only a scoop of water compared to back then.

A slender finger holding a chess piece, hesitating to move, quietly observing this state is enough to be enchanting. If I must win, I'm afraid there is no such villain in the world.

The ancients taught women to sing and dance, not to teach singing and dancing, but to practice their voice and appearance. If you want their voice to be gentle and melodious, you must make them learn to sing. Once they have learned to sing, then every utterance will have the charm of a swallow's song and an oriole's cry. They don't have to sing, but the singing is in it. If you want their posture to be light and graceful, you must make them learn to dance. Once they are skilled in dancing, then every turn and step will be full of the appearance of willows swaying and flowers smiling. They don't have to dance, but the dancing is in it.

These kinds of women have different names depending on the region: in Guangdong, they are called "Lao Ju" (transliteration), in Sichuan they are called "She Wu," in the north they are called "Biao Zi," in northern Huai they are called "Xiang Gong" (this Xiang Gong is not that Xiang Gong), and in Shanghai they are called "Ye Ji." At the same time, they have different categories due to different prices and registries. For example, cheap ones are called "Ban Tiao" in the north, "Che Huo" (transliteration) in Guangdong, "Tu Fei" in northern Huai, and "Shi Peng" in Sichuan; high-priced ones are called "Gu Niang" in the north, "Xiao Jie" in Guangdong, "Pi Pa Zai" in Guangxi, and "Wan Jia" in Sichuan; others include "Shi Bang" and "Guang Bang," which are also distinguished by local characteristics. Shanghai has the most names and grades

Page 20

Shanghai has the most names and grades. Besides "Shu Yu" and "Yun Er," there are also "Ye Ji," "Tang Bai," "Xian Shui Mei," "Xian Rou Zhuang," etc.; while in other places, there are only "First-Class Companies" (also known as "Chang San Tang Zi"), "Second-Class Companies," or "Yang Bang" and "Tu Bang."

Chinese prostitutes can be divided into two major branches, namely "Yangzhou Bang" and "Suzhou Bang." Both have a long history and a solid reputation. We can often see records of Yangzhou and Suzhou prostitutes in novels. For example, Shen Sanbai, the author of "Six Records of a Floating Life," mentioned in "Quick Notes of a Rambling Journey" that he had a good relationship with a Yangzhou prostitute in Guangzhou, which shows that Yangzhou prostitutes had become "crusaders" in the south during the Qianlong era. At that time, the sea route to the south was not yet open to wheeled vehicles, and it had to be transferred from Anhui and Jiangxi. The road was so circuitous and dangerous, and there were still traces of "crusaders," so the rest of the north and west were even more conquered by them. As for Suzhou Bang, they also developed outward very early, and their beautiful names are known in all provinces. However, now Yangzhou Bang still has a relatively large territory and a more prosperous business. They have forces in almost all places: such as the Liangguang region in the Pearl River Basin, where there is no Suzhou Bang, but the forces of Yangzhou Bang are very active; even remote provinces such as Yunnan, Guizhou, and Sichuan have their seductive flags, but they are not called Yangzhou Bang here, but "Xiajiang Gu Niang." As for the places through which the Pinghan, Jinpu, and Longhai railways pass, they are almost all controlled by Yangzhou Bang, and there is a general feeling of accumulated Chen goods in the area. In these places, as long as you see a fashionable woman, if you ask her, "Where is this girl from?" she will definitely answer with a smile, "Yangzhou, a small place." If you ask three or five, the answer is the same. As for Suzhou Bang, their territory has shrunk to only three places: Shanghai, Wuhan, and Beiping. At the same time, these places are also divided by Yangzhou Bang and other parties, but although the territory is small, the business is very developed, because these places are all prosperous big cities, and there are many rich men who spend thousands of dollars to buy a smile, so they are not a weak minority compared to Yangzhou Bang.

In fact, there is not much difference between the two factions. As far as people are concerned, they are all complete with five senses, and the places where they grow up are not very far apart. The so-called "water color" is still about the same. At the same time, there are also those who are originally from Suzhou but are listed as Yangzhou Bang, and vice versa. Originally, Yangzhou Bang and Suzhou Bang were not entirely the products of Yangzhou and Suzhou. As far as I know, many of the Yangzhou Bang girls in Henan are from Hubei; Huaibei is only a short distance from Yangzhou, and half of the Yangzhou Bang there are from Zhenjiang and Anhui; even the Suzhou Bang in Shanghai has many Northerners. The reason why they pretend to be brands is nothing more than to develop their business, because the legend that Suzhou and Yangzhou produce beauties has been circulating for a long time. They think that by carrying such a brand, they will also have the demeanor of a beauty, so you carry this brand and I carry this brand, making all the prostitutes in the country Suzhou Bang or Yangzhou Bang.

The fact is exactly like this; with these two brands, it seems that the price will be particularly noble. Leaving aside Suzhou Bang, let's just talk about Yangzhou Bang. The value of the places they go to is always much higher than that of Tu Bang. For example, in Huaibei, the most a general local prostitute can charge for a night is four or five yuan (even as little as eight corners), while the minimum for a Yangzhou Bang is sixteen yuan. On the Pinghan Road, it can be reduced by three or four yuan, while a Tu Tiao only needs one or two yuan! As for Liangguang and Yunnan, Guizhou, and Sichuan, local goods are even more worthless, while Yangzhou Bang must be at least thirty or forty yuan, and also have to go through "calling Tiao Zi," "doing flower head" and various procedures before "falling into a relationship." These also require tens of yuan in expenses, totaling almost one hundred yuan. Compared, there is a world of difference!

However, they cannot become capitalists. One reason is that the expenses are too large. For example, opening a dish head and laying out a market surface will cost a lot. Second, they have very few customers. It is rare to have two customers a month, because in inland cities (Yangzhou Bang runs mostly foreign docks), there are very few who are willing to spend money like dirt, and there are many people engaged in this business, and the competition is fierce, so their business is getting worse and worse. Last year, when I was on the Pinghan Road, I knew that there were several Yangzhou Bang brothels. Because they had very few customers, in order to maintain their expenses, they advertised to railway staff, voluntarily canceling the procedure of doing flower heads and reducing the cost of the night, in order to attract a few more customers, but the result was still a deserted door, with empty hopes. Several even moved their docks, running to Tongguan and Lanzhou, hoping to find another way out in those remote places. There were also two brothels, because the business was bad, the pimps abused the prostitutes as much as possible, and they even ran to the "Jiliang Institute" to ask for relief. There are even more prostitutes in Huaibei. A reporter from Da Gong Bao said a few years ago that it was a "den of prostitutes." As far as I know, there are more than 200 Yangzhou Bang in Haizhou City and Xinpu Town alone. There are dozens or hundreds in Guanyun County (Banpu) and its affiliated Xiangshui Port, Xugou (Lianyungang is here), and Qingpu Town in Ganyu. In short, the total number of Yangzhou Bang prostitutes in Huaibei is about 1,000, not including Tu Bang. No matter whether it is in the countryside or in the city, you can always find many women wearing rouge and red clothes, and they are all Tu Chang. Now that the floods have almost submerged the entire Huaibei, it is not only the Yangzhou Bang who are looking for food and opening new docks, but also the Tu Bang who have to leave their hometown and live a truly "Jianghu life," and perhaps they will have to borrow the brand of Yangzhou Bang! It is a pity that this brand is already old and can no longer attract buyers!

Literary Works

Raising Relief Funds Ledger (6)

— Pu Yu

"According to

×× Province Stamp Tax and Liquor Bureau Instruction No. 355: "According to the joint confidential report from liquor merchants ××××× and others: Yuan Tai Distillery in Shuanglong Town, under the jurisdiction of the branch, has been brewing liquor for months without reporting it and secretly selling it locally at reduced prices, hindering the market of the same industry, etc. If it is not false, Yuan Tai Distillery is stealing and evading national taxes and despising tax regulations, which is extremely illegal, and the head of the branch is not without blame for failing to supervise. In addition to sending personnel from this bureau to secretly investigate, it is urgently ordered that the head of the branch truthfully investigate and report within three days of receiving the document to facilitate verification, and cut it off." Because: Upon receiving this, it is urgently ordered that the director, Liu Pi, go to Yuan Tai Distillery on a set date to extract the account books, find out how much liquor the distillery brews daily, how much it sells, and whether the total quantity is consistent with the excise tax certificate used, and truthfully report it to the bureau for verification. If the Yuan Tai Distillery dares to resist and refuse to hand over the accounts, the director should first seal off the mouth of the distillery cellar and consult with the local military police to escort the distillery owner to the bureau..."

I finished reading the imperial decree aloud and showed him the place where the seal was stamped, then carefully locked the Zhu Dan in the leather bag!

But the old thing didn't have much ability. At this time, his eyes were stunned with fright, his whole body was trembling, and his loyal face became a pitiful look. I secretly prepared myself, I shouldn't have gone so far. But for the temptation of money, what can I do?

At this time, in my eyes, he was just like a wounded dog. He didn't have the courage to resist. He was afraid that others would attack him again. But I went further, secretly giving Jiang Xiwu an order; that kid was very smart, and immediately showed his power, putting on a man-eating posture:

"Hey, Boss Li, if you want to save face, take out the account book yourself. I can seal the cellar mouth for you!"

"……!" The old man looked at me with a crying face, his nerves confused.

"Hurry up! Official business is urgent." I put on a stern face and said this sentence, then crossed my right leg over my left leg.

The old man almost shed tears, and after a long daze, he moved half a step at a time to my side, pursed his lips and blurted out a crying voice, "Director, please discuss it again." He looked at my face again: "Our merchant's account book cannot be separated from it for a moment. If it is taken away, then... reputation, faith, business, will all be... that! Even the wine vat cannot be righted. If it really is... then the loss will be great!"

Damn it, he still wants to say it. I knew a long time ago that doing this would scare him half to death. But, I didn't let go immediately, deliberately putting on a strong bear attitude, speaking in a decisive tone:

"No! Official business cannot be negotiated!"

The old man immediately showed a disappointed look, frowning tightly and sighing for a long time. I felt that he was just like a dog bound by others. I was preparing the knife, slowly bleeding, peeling, and cutting meat!

Finally, talking about the "number" was a bloody battle. I wanted to fight for more, but the old man cried and begged to reduce it. His reason—actually, it could be a plea; the distillery lost money, the expenses were too high, and there was no money... What I made up was: the case was serious, and it would not be possible to spend more money. In the end, I said in a half-threatening, half-persuasive tone:

The following continues on page five

Page 21

"You have to understand that this is an order from the provincial bureau. Although our branch can report that there is no theft or corruption, it will still send a committee member to investigate. For the committee member, the reception fee alone will cost more than one hundred yuan, and to prevent him from saying bad things, will it cost a few dollars? You must know that other people who handle official business are definitely not as kind and soft-spoken as I am. Also, those in our bureau who handle paperwork, stay up all night for your affairs, don't they need a few tea money? To be honest, if I, Lao Liu, had bad intentions, I would be cut off from my descendants."

As soon as I finished saying the four words "cut off from my descendants," I felt a chill in my heart, and Jiang Xiwu, that hateful kid, "choked" out a laugh. Damn it, he almost made my face blush! I glared at him fiercely before putting on a peaceful face and saying to the old man:

"Boss Li, I, Liu, am a good friend. I want to help to the end. But, as you know, I don't have the power to give money. In short, four hundred yuan is not much, otherwise, then..." I didn't say the second half of the sentence definitively, just shook my head slightly a couple of times! (To be continued)

Movie News

"One Night of Tenderness" Released

Paramount's "One Night of Tenderness" Hands Acoss The Tabl, starring beauty star Carole Lombard, is a romantic and passionate blockbuster comparable to "It Happened One Night." The film tells the story of a man and a woman, one wanting to marry a wealthy son, and the other wanting to marry a wealthy woman; but taking advantage of their loneliness, they live together, and when the night is quiet, they express their passion. In the end, love triumphs over money, and they both abandon their vanity and become lifelong partners. This film uses a very delicate approach to portray the feelings between men and women, which is quite touching. The film has been released at the Great Light Cinema today. The picture is a scene from "One Night of Tenderness."

Silver Jottings

— Zhi Er

The daughter of "Standard Beauty," Xiao Feng, died of diphtheria. Will "Standard Beauty" have no descendants? (Note: "No descendants" refers to "Standard Beauty" having no descendants, not Xu Lai having no descendants.)

Hu Die's wedding newsreel has been shown in Jincheng before "Boat Girl" in the past few days. The reason why "Boat Girl" had Hu Die's wedding newsreel a few days ago was due to the incomplete review procedures.

It is also rumored that "Boat Girl" was originally scheduled to be shown after Shanghai Company's "Peach Blossom Dream," but it was temporarily moved forward. The "cover advertisement" issue is related to this; in fact, Shen Xiling would never argue about this.

New Era Company's "Mr. Wang Goes to the Countryside" was secretly screened at the Central Grand Theater at 12:00 last night.

It is unknown whether the star's "blockbuster" "Begonia Red" will be starred by Bai Yushuang? It is rumored that the script was personally written by Zhang Shichuan, but this is not true. The script was actually written by Mr. Wang "Superficial".

It is rumored that Miss Liang Baipi, who is related to Ye Qianyu's disappearance, has been very interested in dancing recently and has been seen in various nightclubs. Some say: "After Qianyu, here is another one."

Who exactly is Jiang Jianxia?

When this name appeared in "Modern" and "Literary Pictorial," it was indeed Du Heng's old shop, but in an article signed Jiang Jianxia in the later "Morning Light," it talked about the feud between Du Heng and Mao Dun, so some people suspected it was Ye Lingfeng's pseudonym. Yesterday, "Crossroads" stated that Jiang Jianxia was the pen name of Ye Lingfeng and Mu Shiying, so this "hybrid" should specifically refer to "Wu Jianxia" in "Morning Light" and "Daily Movies".

"Hero of the Times" to be screened today

"Hero of the Times" is a problem drama dissecting the reasons for the decline of commerce and industry. It is the latest and most valuable sound production of Yihua Company, and it is Ying Yunwei's carefully crafted masterpiece of the year. The set designer is Fang Peilin, the sound engineer is Gu Zongyi, and the leading actors include Shang Guanwu, Jiang Xiu, Ma Loufen, Ye Juanjuan, Zhang Zhizhi, Wang Naidong, Qin Tong, Wan Laitian, Hu Ping, Zhang Wen, etc. This film is scheduled to be publicly screened at the Jincheng Grand Theater at 10:00 AM today (the 8th), and the official release date will be within the next few days. Anyone who cares about domestic films must see it.
